			new_tempo0{real} := new_tempo00{real}
			i0{int} := i00{int}
			ii0{int} := ii00{int}
			iii0{int} := iii00{int}
				new_tempo0{real} := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / 960
				if((new_tempo0{real} # tempo{real}) or (NI_CALLBACK_TYPE{int} # NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER{int}))
					i0{int} := 0
					ii0{int} := 0
					iii0{int} := 0
					i0{int} := 0
					while(i0{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
						ii0{int} := 0
						while(ii0{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
							iii0{int} := 0
							while(iii0{int} <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} - 1)) 
								if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(i0{int} * 32) + ((ii0{int} * 4) + iii0{int})]{int}]{int}]{int} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{int})
									_repetition_interval_time[(i0{int} * 4096) + ((ii0{int} * 512) + iii0{int})]{int} := int((60000 / new_tempo0{real}) * (4 / real(_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[(i0{int} * 32) + ((ii0{int} * 4) + iii0{int})]{int}){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
								end if
								inc(iii0{int}){Builtin, None}
							end while
							inc(ii0{int}){Builtin, None}
						end while
						inc(i0{int}){Builtin, None}
					end while
					tempo{real} := new_tempo0{real}
				end if

															set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_category[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
														else
															set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_category[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
														end if
														inc(i22{int}){Builtin, None}
													end while
													subarticulation_browser_active_category{int} := category00{int}



									end if



					end if
				end if

on ui_control(xy_center_circles{real[]}){thread-unsafe}
	cc_cb_id{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int})
				ret15{real} := distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
				x17{real} := xy_center_circles[0]{real}
				y3{real} := xy_center_circles[1]{real}
				new_tempo00{real} := new_tempo00{real}
				dy0{real} := dy00{real}
				call center_circle_distance{UserDefined, Call}


				ret16{real} := angle2[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
				x18{real} := xy_center_circles[0]{real}
				y4{real} := xy_center_circles[1]{real}
				new_tempo00{real} := new_tempo00{real}
				dy00{real} := dy00{real}
				cos_theta0{real} := cos_theta00{real}
				angle1{real} := angle10{real}
				call center_circle_angle{UserDefined, Call}


				ret17{int} := controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
				angle0{real} := angle2[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
				angle_min0{real} := 0.7
				angle_max0{real} := (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2) - 0.7
				dy00{real} := dy00{real}
				call angle_to_value{UserDefined, Call}


		if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.32) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.36))
			selected_subarticulation{int} := 0
		else
			if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.36) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.4))
				selected_subarticulation{int} := 1
			else
				if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.4) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.44))
					selected_subarticulation{int} := 2
				else
					if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.44) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.48))
						selected_subarticulation{int} := 3
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end if
		if(abs(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} < 10)
			selected_circle_end{int} := 0
		else
			if(abs(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} < 10)
				selected_circle_end{int} := 1
			else
				selected_circle_end{int} := - 1
			end if
		end if
				offset100{int} := offset100{int}
				call update_subarticulation_selection{UserDefined, Call}


	end if
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG{int})
		wait(10000){Builtin, None}
		if((cc_cb_id{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}) and (selected_circle_end{int} # - 1))
					ret16{real} := angle2[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
					x18{real} := xy_center_circles[0]{real}
					y4{real} := xy_center_circles[1]{real}
					dy00{real} := dy00{real}
					new_tempo00{real} := new_tempo00{real}
					cos_theta00{real} := cos_theta00{real}
					angle10{real} := angle10{real}
					call center_circle_angle{UserDefined, Call}


					ret17{int} := controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
					angle0{real} := angle2[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
					angle_min0{real} := 0.7
					angle_max0{real} := (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2) - 0.7
					angle10{real} := angle10{real}
					call angle_to_value{UserDefined, Call}


			if(selected_circle_end{int} = 0)
				if(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} < ((_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}) - _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}))
					_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
				end if
			else
				if(selected_circle_end{int} = 1)
					if(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} > ((_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} + _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}) + _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}))
						_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
					end if
				end if
			end if
				call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, Call}

				call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, Call}

		end if
	end if
end on

			uiid00{int} := btn_mixer_channel_enable[4]{int}

			i1700{int} := i110000{int}
			ii410{int} := result7000{int}
			iii110{int} := i12000{int}
			_ret660010{int} := end_note200{int}
			group_count00010{int} := transition_type200{int}
			group_count00110{int} := transition_note000{int}
				idx270{int} := search[sli_mixer_channel_volume{int[]}, uiid00{int}]
				if(idx270{int} # - 1)
					set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME{int}, get_control_par(sli_mixer_channel_volume[idx270{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None}, - 1, - 1, NI_BUS_OFFSET{int} + idx270{int}){Builtin, None}
					if(idx270{int} = 4)
						set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME{int}, get_control_par(sli_mixer_channel_volume[idx270{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None}, - 1, - 1, NI_BUS_OFFSET{int} + 5){Builtin, None}
					end if
				end if
				idx270{int} := search[btn_mixer_channel_enable{int[]}, uiid00{int}]
				if(idx270{int} # - 1)
					if(idx270{int} < 4)
						microphone_position_states[idx270{int}]{int} := get_control_par(btn_mixer_channel_enable[idx270{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None}
					else
						microphone_position_states[idx270{int} + mnu_mixer_bleed_channel{int}]{int} := get_control_par(btn_mixer_channel_enable[idx270{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None}
						microphone_position_states[idx270{int} + (1 - mnu_mixer_bleed_channel{int})]{int} := FALSE{int}
					end if
							i17{int} := i1700{int}
							ii4{int} := ii410{int}
							iii1{int} := iii110{int}

function set_background_animation
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_bg{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "bg_ani_" & ((frame0{int} / 32) + 1)){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_bg{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, (frame0{int} mod 32) - (((frame0{int} mod 32) - (30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs((frame0{int} / 32) - 3){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})) .and. sh_right((30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs((frame0{int} / 32) - 3){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}) - (frame0{int} mod 32), 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
end function

function set_key_colors
	i3{int} := 0
	i3{int} := 0
	while(i3{int} <= 127) 
		set_key_color(i3{int}, KEY_COLOR_WHITE{int}){Builtin, None}
		if((i3{int} >= 55) and (i3{int} <= 96))
			set_key_color(i3{int}, KEY_COLOR_BLUE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i3{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function keyswitches_color_keys
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_RED{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} = ON{int})
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_keyswitch_selection

	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "          "){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE{int}, "          "){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE{int}, _articulation_names[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch_purge[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch_purge_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_key_pressed((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
				set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_RED{int}){Builtin, None}
				if(_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} = ON{int})
					set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int}){Builtin, None}
				end if

	selected_subarticulation{int} := 0

				idx1700{int} := idx17000{int}

						btn_articulation_release{int} := OFF{int}
					else

						set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_articulation_release_blocker{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}

					end if
							set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}

							i{int} := 0

function articulations_compute_level
	subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := 0
	fade_in_start0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_start[(instrument_slot2{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch3{int} * 4) + subarticulation2{int})]{int}
	fade_in_range0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(instrument_slot2{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch3{int} * 4) + subarticulation2{int})]{int}
	fade_out_end0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_end[(instrument_slot2{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch3{int} * 4) + subarticulation2{int})]{int}
	fade_out_range0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(instrument_slot2{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch3{int} * 4) + subarticulation2{int})]{int}
	if(in_range(modulation_positions[note6{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, fade_in_start0{int}, fade_out_end0{int}){Builtin, None})
		subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := 1
		if(in_range(modulation_positions[note6{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, fade_in_start0{int}, fade_in_start0{int} + fade_in_range0{int}){Builtin, None} and (fade_in_range0{int} > 0))
			subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := real(modulation_positions[note6{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} - fade_in_start0{int}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_in_range0{int}){Builtin, None}

function repetition_engine_add

		end if

function last_transitions_update
	i11{int} := 0
	i11{int} := 0
	while(i11{int} <= (num_elements[_last_transitions{int[]}] - 1)) 
		if(_last_transitions[i11{int}]{int} # - 1)
			if(_last_transitions_timecode[i11{int}]{int} < (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - 2000))
				_last_transitions[i11{int}]{int} := - 1
			end if
		end if
		inc(i11{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function last_transitions_contains
	result7{int} := FALSE{int}
	i12{int} := 0
			i11{int} := i110{int}
			call last_transitions_update{UserDefined, Call}


	i12{int} := 0
	while(i12{int} <= 7) 
		if(_last_transitions[(instrument3{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch2{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx2{int} * 8) + i12{int}))]{int} = ((128 * transition_type1{int}) + note3{int}))
			result7{int} := TRUE{int}
			_last_transitions[(instrument3{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch2{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx2{int} * 8) + i12{int}))]{int} := - 1
		end if
		inc(i12{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	ret13{int} := result7{int}
end function

function last_transitions_add_event
	idx24{int} := - 1
	min3{int} := _last_transitions_timecode[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + (subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8))]{int}
	min_idx0{int} := 0
	i13{int} := 0
	if(transition_type0{int} >= 0)
		i13{int} := 0
		while(i13{int} <= 7) 
			if(_last_transitions[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + i13{int}))]{int} = - 1)
				idx24{int} := i13{int}
				if(min3{int} > _last_transitions_timecode[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + i13{int}))]{int})
					min3{int} := _last_transitions_timecode[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + i13{int}))]{int}
					min_idx0{int} := i13{int}
				end if
			end if
			inc(i13{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(idx24{int} # - 1)
			_last_transitions[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + idx24{int}))]{int} := (128 * transition_type0{int}) + note2{int}
			_last_transitions_timecode[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + idx24{int}))]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		else
			_last_transitions[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + min_idx0{int}))]{int} := (128 * transition_type0{int}) + note2{int}
			_last_transitions_timecode[(instrument2{int} * 256) + ((keyswitch1{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_idx1{int} * 8) + min_idx0{int}))]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		end if
	end if
end function

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} # - 1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int}]{int}]{int} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{int})
			authoring_page_active{int} := TRUE{int}
			set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_authoring_legato_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int}]{int}]{string} & " (" & _loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} & ")"){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function authoring_open
		call find_loaded_legato{UserDefined, Call}

			start_note0{int} := 60
			end_note0{int} := 60
			dynamic_layer0{int} := 0
			call update_authoring_transition{UserDefined, Call}


	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_authoring{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_subarticulation_selection
				_iter0{int} := 0
				while(_iter0{int} <= (num_elements(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection{int[]}){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
					ui_array2[_iter0{int}]{int[]} := btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[_iter0{int}]{int[]}
					inc(_iter0{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while

			exception_idx1{int} := selected_subarticulation{int}
			idx17{int} := idx170{int}
				idx17{int} := 0
				idx17{int} := 0
				while(idx17{int} <= (num_elements[ui_array2{int[]}] - 1)) 
					if(idx17{int} # exception_idx1{int})
						set_control_par(ui_array2[idx17{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
					else
						set_control_par(ui_array2[idx17{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
					end if
					inc(idx17{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while



	if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} # - 1)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "    " & subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}]{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
	else
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "    Empty"){Builtin, None}
	end if
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_solo_subarticulation{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _subarticulations_solo_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}

function subarticulation_browser_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} # - 1)
				category00{int} := type_to_category[subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}
				i22{int} := i20{int}
					i22{int} := 0
					i22{int} := 0
					while(i22{int} <= (num_elements[btn_subarticulation_browser_selection{int[]}] - 1)) 
						set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
						if(_subarticulation_browser_entries[(category00{int} * 14) + i22{int}]{int} # - 1)
							set_control_par_str(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_subarticulation_browser_entries[(category00{int} * 14) + i22{int}]{int}]{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
							if(_subarticulation_browser_entries[(category00{int} * 14) + i22{int}]{int} = _loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int})
								set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
							else
								set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
							end if
							set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
						end if
						inc(i22{int}){Builtin, None}
					end while
					i22{int} := 0
					while(i22{int} <= (num_elements[btn_subarticulation_browser_category{int[]}] - 1)) 
						if(i22{int} = category00{int})
							set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_category[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
						else
							set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_category[i22{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
						end if
						inc(i22{int}){Builtin, None}
					end while
					subarticulation_browser_active_category{int} := category00{int}



	end if
end function

function subarticulation_browser_close
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_max[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_curve[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int} * - 1){Builtin, None}
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}] - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}, int(round(real(int((real(_articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} + (real(int((real(_articulation_volume_max[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None} - int((real(_articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} * pow(real(i{int}){Builtin, None} / real(num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}]){Builtin, None}, (real(_articulation_volume_curve[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while

function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int} # - 1)
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			if(i{int} = selected_subarticulation{int})
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			else
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, 127 - _loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_dynamic_range_control
	xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127

	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
			modwheel3{int} := modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}
				set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_cursor{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - 5) + int((real(((modwheel3{int} * (1 + (sh_right(127 - modwheel3{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(modwheel3{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (1 * sh_right(modwheel3{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})) - (127 * sh_right(127 - modwheel3{int}, 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}



end function

function center_circle_distance
	dx0{real} := x17{real} - 0.5
	dy0{real} := y3{real} - 0.5
	ret15{real} := sqrt((dx0{real} * dx0{real}) + (dy0{real} * dy0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_angle
	dx1{real} := x18{real} - 0.5
	dy1{real} := y4{real} - 0.5
	cos_theta0{real} := dx1{real} / sqrt((dx1{real} * dx1{real}) + (dy1{real} * dy1{real})){Builtin, None}
	angle1{real} := acos(cos_theta0{real}){Builtin, None}
	if(dy1{real} < 0)
		angle1{real} := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real}) - angle1{real}
	end if
	ret16{real} := angle1{real}
end function

function angle_to_value
	new_angle0{real} := angle0{real} + (NI_MATH_PI{real} / 2)
	if(new_angle0{real} > (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2))
		new_angle0{real} := new_angle0{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})
	end if
	new_angle0{real} := abs(new_angle0{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})){Builtin, None}
	ret17{int} := int((127 * (new_angle0{real} - angle_min0{real})) / (angle_max0{real} - angle_min0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function move_to_legato_buffer

	note_idx1{int} := 0
	transition_idx1{int} := 0
	dyn_layer_idx1{int} := 0
	while(dyn_layer_idx1{int} <= (MAX_TRANSITION_DYN_LAYERS{int} - 1)) 
		note_idx1{int} := 0
		while(note_idx1{int} <= 127) 
			transition_idx1{int} := 0
			while(transition_idx1{int} <= (MAX_TRANSITIONS_PER_NOTE{int} - 1)) 
				_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[(dyn_layer_idx1{int} * 3200) + ((note_idx1{int} * 25) + transition_idx1{int})]{int} := _legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[(instrument8{int} * 204800) + ((keyswitch12{int} * 25600) + ((subarticulation_idx6{int} * 6400) + ((dyn_layer_idx1{int} * 3200) + ((note_idx1{int} * 25) + transition_idx1{int}))))]{int}
				_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[(dyn_layer_idx1{int} * 3200) + ((note_idx1{int} * 25) + transition_idx1{int})]{int} := _legato_data_sus_release_time[(instrument8{int} * 204800) + ((keyswitch12{int} * 25600) + ((subarticulation_idx6{int} * 6400) + ((dyn_layer_idx1{int} * 3200) + ((note_idx1{int} * 25) + transition_idx1{int}))))]{int}
